Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude; puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine; puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz; puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine; se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre; et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit; et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier; puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi; ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit; et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And if the appearance is in the intestine or bladder, then you should command the patient to tighten his belt and be stretched out straight, then sign all around the stomach; then command him to lie still between your hands, then go around the place that you have marked on the whole spasm, then extend half of the abscess above the great fingernail; then tie it tightly all around with a strong thread or strong silk cord, and let the patient's nose be free from the rope; then work half of the abscess extended over the rope, and put in your finger, and seek the intestine; if you find it caught by the rope, release it and pull out the intestine from the abdomen; and if you find the bladder, grab it at the nail and cut off the excess; and if the artery or vein makes a noise, go around smoothly, then return to your work and take two needles, and thread them with two strong threads, and pass the needles through what you made in a cross so that you make a piercing; then draw out the abscess in four places on the needles, and when you see it, remove the needles and let the place heal as it can, and cut away the dead flesh by itself; or scrape it when it becomes thin and healable, then cure the wound as needed, and close the wound.
dou chancre	from a ulcer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer; et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement; et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner; ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	We have discussed the types of ulcers and how to treat them with medicine, as well as the importance of cauterization with iron. Now, let us speak of the ulceration that occurs in the mouth, and the great caution that must be taken in its treatment. The ancients said that when an ulcer is in a place where it can be reached, such as in the breast or armpit, and in similar places, it should all be removed when it is in its early stages. However, once it becomes large and old, one must not touch it, for I have never seen anyone heal from this.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire; puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide .i. boin leu por faire l’ovraige; puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier; et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the work, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you sometimes purge the patient of black bile; then let him bleed if he has manifest fullness, then open the disease in a suitable place to perform the operation; then cut your fingernails or calluses, and the skin all over, and the bone all over without leaving anything; and let the blood flow out completely, and squeeze the site well with your hand or something, and if the bleeding from the incision of the artery or vein makes you feel faint, cauterize it until the bleeding stops; then treat it with other remedies until it heals.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer: lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	We have already discussed in the division the appearances of dropsy and how the accumulation of fluid occurs, along with the signs of each appearance, the treatment through medication, and that which is cured by iron. Only this much; one should not use iron for these two types of dropsy: tympanites and yposarche, as they are fatal conditions. Therefore, when treating this type of dropsy called "eclites" with medications and the cure does not help, consider if the patient is weak or has other illnesses besides dropsy, such as stomach issues and similar conditions; then one should not use iron, as there is a risk involved. But if you see that the patient is strong and has only dropsy, and is neither too young nor too old, then you should proceed as follows: lift the patient straight up, and have an assistant press on the abdomen to push the fluid towards the lowest part of the feet. Then, take the spatha (a type of knife) with a serrated edge and proceed in this manner:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let there be two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier; puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu; puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	And let there be two parts. a point, and yet not so sharp that it can pierce the intestines when you insert it, nor bleed; then look to see if the dropsy is in the intestines: then you should split under the armpit on the right side; and if the disease is the liver, then the split should be on the left side of the armpit; and it is not good for the patient to lie on the split so that the superfluities do not flow into that weak place; then pierce all the way through the skin with the instrument, and plug it up, and leave your hand at the whole spatumile between the skin and the syringe as you would when skinning, to the amount of a fingernail or more; then pierce the syringe so that the spatumile comes out at the desired place, and this is where the water will come out; then pull it out, and plug up this instrument with what it is made of:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus; et II d’autre part, et I d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	It resembles a silver-colored wire, made of thin bronze or light iron, with a small hole in the lower part. On one side there are three holes, on another two, and on another one, and the head is shaped like a feather, cut in the form of an incision that scribes use to shape feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort; mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit; fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	above the tip is the funnel, so that when the instrument comes to a boil, it is drawn up immediately into the instrument; therefore empty half or a third of it, for if you empty more than is appropriate in that hour, by chance the patient may die from the shock to his spirit due to the instrument, or he may faint, or he may approach death; but empty according to the quantity of his strength, and according to what the dispositions of his strength indicate, and his pulses; then withdraw the instrument and hold the vessel steady, and now it is retained by the membrane which blocks the hole above the syphiac, about which I have spoken, that you pierce in this manner; then reintroduce the instrument the next day if you see the patient bearing it, and draw a small quantity of water; do this each day, and beware of overdoing it until there is only a little water left.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	If you doubt the illness and leave it a lot of water, then cure with hot sand or ash, and with much sweating or bathing in the sun; and if it is dyed by drinking, cure with medicines that dry up until he is healed, and cauterize on the stomach and liver and spleen after the extraction of water, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the stopping of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without a foreskin, or with a small one, or it is not in its place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If necessary, he should pierce the foreskin with a very thin needle according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Then put a thin piece of lead in the foreskin and ligature it, and hold it thus for three or four days, and when he wants to urinate, remove the ligature, and urinate, and then put it back; and perhaps this is not necessary at all, because the urine that comes out does not allow the foreskin to close.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those whose foreskin is tight, if it is treated with the cautery of lead, as we have said, will loosen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	Those who do not have the foreskin in its place are blighted, for some are born with the foreskin at the tip of the penis, which prevents them from urinating until they lift their penis upward; and they cannot ejaculate because the material cannot reach the glans, and this is a serious ailment.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the method of treatment is that the patient lies on his back, then the tip and glans of the penis are cut to the size of a feather, so that the foreskin splits in the middle, as it should be; and beware of bleeding which often occurs, and if it does, stop the blood flow with something that stops blood flow, and treat the wound until it heals.
des pustules de la verge	of pustules on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times, there are boils on the penis, and it is an ugly skin appearance; and there are both benign and malignant ones; so you must cut them to a depth of one-eighth inch, then scrape and clean all of them, then put cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment over them; then cure with thin ointment until it heals.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the foreskin is malignant, discolored and putrid, then you must apply the cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	When you have cut it, and if the foreskin is inside the penis, and part of it is within the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the foreskin that is inside; and when it is healed, then cure the part that is outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	For when you heal it together, if the foreskin is not secure and piercing occurs, then blackness and corruption arise in his penis and scrotum; so you must cut off all that is black and corrupted, then apply the ointment of honey and flour made from pomegranate rinds and walnuts, then heal it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is bleeding, administer the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars; et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	The cauteries are of two types: for bleeding and for corruption; and if the foreskin is swollen and drawn back, you must boil the end of the penis with lead in water, and the patient must urinate through it; and if there is pain at the tip of the penis due to a wound or an abscess, then you must cut it with an instrument, so that the skin splits, and the foreskin is freed from all around, and the head of the penis is delivered from all parts; and if it is difficult to speak of this, then you must cut it with a spatulum at some spot on the tip of the penis and the glans; then gently pull them apart and place a thin damp linen cloth between them that has been dipped in cold water so that it does not become erect again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not dislocation of continuity like other wounds; nevertheless when we perform this act of our own will, and properly on children, it is necessary that we make the best and lightest wound for their safety.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not circumcise their children, for they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen the greatest part of masters and surgeons who circumcised around the glans, and with force, and all over the foreskin; so the head would go out because there are two membranes, and by chance one is above and the other below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Then they bandage it, and the pain is doubled, and in the purification which is done from below, the joint of the member is not set right; and in the purification of the nail, perhaps the iron escapes, and they ruin the work, and many times they grow thus so that they do not need purification and I want it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the purification which is done with force throughout all the thread I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly as well above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues; puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien; et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge; puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because when you press your hand, you cut evenly into it all around; but the thread should be well tied around the skin; and the manner of the first work is such that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the rod, and then you make him move in every way you can; then you make him stand between your hands straight up, and keep the forces between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, or any of the instruments; then you put your hand on the rod and breathe or kiss it, and pull it up until the head of the rod is in; then cleanse it well of the filth that has accumulated there, then tie the place marked with a double thread, then tie it under I to the other string; and hold it by the second string with your thumb and index finger, and press between the two strings, then lift the skin gently and pull the head of the rod; then let the blood flow little by little, for that is the disease; and put powder on top of the powder, a cloth glued with an egg cooked in rosewater, infused with good fresh rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, and heal it with another healing until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The form of the force for purification is as follows: the two cheeks should be thin and sharp, and the ears as big as the hands, equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	the error of purification is when the wound within bleeds; therefore, you must stretch it with your fingernail, so that the pus makes an abscess; and the scabs likewise, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then hold it with tweezers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it persists for 3 days, and what is under the foreskin is swollen, then let it be until the abscesses are soothed and the scabs lightly peeled; then cut it as much as you can, and be careful of the part of the foreskin, it will not harm him in any way.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore treat the site of sudden injuries with a poultice, as we have said in the treatise on poultices, and if it oozes pus excessively, do not wipe it away, but let it flow; then treat it as we have said until it heals.
dou retenement de l’urine	from retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The retention of urine is due to a stone, or congealed blood, or an obstruction, or a growth, or similar causes that we have mentioned in the previous section. If the urine is not released and you see the obstruction caused by the stone lodged in the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent over at the waist with his feet on his back, stretching his abdomen from above the back, and straining as hard as he can; this will force the neck of the bladder upwards to expel the stone, thus releasing the urine. If this does not work as described, and the patient experiences great pain, then you must use a tool called a "syringe", made as follows: it should be crafted from thin silver, like the feather of a bird; the tube should be about a palm and a half in length, with a slender end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the way to pass urine is that you take a double thread and tie it to the end of some wool or cotton, and put the end of the thread into the syringe; and compress the excess wool and put it up to the end of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or lard and egg yolk, and make the patient sit on a chair, and raise his bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water; then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then tie the penis above towards the scrotum; then fill the syringe up to the bladder, and feel the patient's bladder being emptied, and if this is not done according to this order, then the person guiding where it goes is wrong; then pull out the thread all the way through the wool, and the urine follows the wool, then pull it out, and let the urine flow; and repeat the syringe until the bladder is empty and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or bleeding occurs in the bladder, or when pus gathers there, and you see water and medicine dripping out, then do this to all of the instrument which is called 'clepsydra', and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed, and has three openings: two on one side, and one on the other, as you can see; and the hair-like channels through which the medicine flows should be such that it blocks the penis without addition, so that one can withdraw moisture, and push when necessary; and when you see your medicines moving in the bladder, place the tip of the syringe in the moisture, and draw while pulling the plunger out; thus you will draw moisture into the syringe, and then push the plunger in strongly; the moisture will enter the syringe, and come to the bladder at once, so that the patient feels it; and this is the form of the subtle enema with which one enemas the bladder: thus it is:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is made of silver or brass, and the head is higher; and under it has a testicle or both testicles hanging; then take a bladder of mutton and put the moisture in which you wish to enema the bladder, then tie it between the two testicles formed of a good double thread, and heat this moisture over the fire; then push the tip of the enema into the penis, then squeeze your hand over the bladder gently, until the patient feels that the moisture has come to the bladder; and if you do not have a bladder, then take a piece of parchment, and make it into a circle, and pierce it all around; then tie the thread tightly in these openings, then assemble the circle as one assembles a lid, and put inside what you wish of oil and moisture and water, and attach it to the instrument; and do as you did with the bladder, by squeezing with your hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	of stones
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division the methods of stone extraction along with medications; and I have described the difference between a stone lodged in the ureter, and all the signs, and on which type of stone one should operate; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the water flows from the bladder similar to water in its subtlety; and it appears as a vein, and the patient feels pain in his penis, and he can urinate many times, and then it swells; and many of these stones have hard cores; and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is fitting first to cleanse the patient with an enema to draw out all the feces that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes blocks the search for the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet and tilt him upside down so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from the upper region; then have him sit between your hands, which are equipped with an appliance, and his hands beneath his thighs so that the bladder is fully tilted downward; then feel around inside; if you sense the stone in the passage, then hurry now to cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not come out with the touch, then moisten your index finger with oil from your left hand, if the patient is fat, or your middle finger if the patient is young and slim; then insert it into his anus, and feel around for the stone, and when you sense it at your finger, draw it toward the neck of the bladder; then press on with your finger, and guide the stone to where you want to cut.Et le piege a tu qu’il ne se mueve pas tant que li piere ne soit taillie.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the assistant to press on the bladder with his hand, and for the patient to extend their testicles upwards with their right hand, and with their left hand pull back the skin underneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum tightly, following its natural shape.
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And they make an incision between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the navel; and it should be straight above the stone, and both fingers should be at the anus, and the incision should be diagonal so that it is wide at the top and narrow at the bottom, according to the size of the stone, not too large; perhaps the pressure of the finger at the anus will cause it to come out without effort; and know that there is a kind of stone that has angles and edges: it is difficult to extract; and there is another kind that is round like a grape, and its extraction is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And for the one with angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not come out, then you must use forceps at the top like a file to extract the stone so that it does not slip away; or you insert a thin instrument under it at the head; and if you cannot capture it thus, then widen the opening and apply vitriolic ointment, and if there is more than one stone, then insert the largest into the neck of the bladder first, then push it out, then the others afterward if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be sutured, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	For there are two things that can happen to the patient: either they die or the urine comes out where the urethra cannot heal; but nevertheless, you must continue to draw it out with tweezers, until you have removed it in pieces; and when you have finished your work, apply incense, aloe, and dragon's blood to the wound, and constrict it, and place a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, on top to soothe the hot abscess; then re-bind the wound on the neck, and do not loosen the ligature until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment, until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if hot abscesses and corrosions come into the wound, and blood congestion in the bladder, and there is retention of urine due to this, which is known in such a way that it comes out with the urine: therefore, insert your finger into the wound and draw out that blood, for if it remains, it will corrupt the bladder and cause it to protrude; then wash the wound with water and garlic and salt, and help him in every way you know how until he is healed; and it is necessary that every hour that you treat him, you bind his two thighs together, and assemble the remedies on the site.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small and lodged in the urethra, piercing it and preventing urine from flowing; then the treatment I have described, which you should cut into many times, is sufficient for this condition.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have tried this successfully.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	And the treatment which is more beneficial to health, then one must cut it as soon as possible, for it cannot stay, and the urine cannot pass; and while it is being cut, he feels great pain, but after it is cut, he feels relief.Take a 1-inch iron rod according to this shape with 3 angles fixed in a tongs:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot move back into the bladder; then insert the drill into the penis gently, until it reaches the stone; and turn the drill in your hand inside the stone, little by little, until you pierce the stone from another side; then urine will flow immediately, press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is broken at once and comes out with the urine, the patient is cured; if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents them, tie a thread under the stone and another above, then push the penis against the stone between the two threads, extract it, untie the thread, and cleanse the congealed blood in the wound; treat until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of stones in women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes lodged in women, and if it does, the cure is difficult, and is prohibited by three things: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a well-informed woman who reveals herself to midwives, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And the third way is that, by chance, one cannot find a woman well-skilled in this art of medicine; and the fourth way is that the stone in a woman is deeper than in a man, so it needs to be cut more deeply, and there is greater fear involved. And if necessity arises, one should press a needle into it, and if one cannot extract it with the needle, then one must use a very fine castor oil; and present to her a wise midwife experienced in the affairs of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you command regarding the inquiry of the stone; and be very careful that the woman is a virgin. Then she should press her finger into the urethra and seek out the stone; and if she finds it, she should hold it firmly beneath her finger, and command her to press her left hand hard upon the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If you find it, then you must move it from the entrance of the bladder all the way down to the root of the thigh; then press on the stone in the root of the thigh towards the middle of the groin, where the testicles are located and feel the stone in that area; do not move your hand above or below the stone, and let the incision be small at first. Then pour water into the incision if you feel the stone has been cut so that it can come out; know that there are many types of stones: small ones, large ones, rough ones, smooth ones, long ones, and round ones, and some have hairs on them.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	You must know their appearances in order to understand the cure.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood comes out, then apply ground vitriol and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your work so that the stone can come out, and have ready the instruments I told you about in extracting stones from men to aid you in your task; and if the blood comes out and it is from the artery that has been cut, then apply the powder to the site and constrict it with bandages and tourniquets, and do not touch that wound again, and leave the stone and do not try to remove it, for the patient might die; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your task and have the stone extracted.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	A watery hernia is nothing other than an accumulation of moisture or white pus, which is located below the membrane of the testicles that contains the egg; and it is called 'pus', and sometimes it is properly in the membrane of the egg, if one believes it to be another egg; and this occurs between the white pus that we mentioned earlier.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the cause of this hernia is due to weakness that affects the testicles, causing this material to accumulate and spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testes, and this moisture has many colors: or it is a yellow shade, or it is red-less, or black, or watery white, and that happens more; and these are the signs of recognizing this assembly, for if it is in the white syphilis that we have said, then the abscesses are re-emerged, a little long as the shape of an egg, and does not appear to the testes, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if there is moisture in the testicle itself, then the abscesses are re-emerged with part of an egg, and because of this one thinks it's another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testes and the white syphilis, it feels good; therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test the entire scrotum, from which the shape is described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this then, what comes after the scrotum, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we treat it with fire, the patient should be bled according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he should lie on his back on something slightly raised, and have a lot of blankets under him; then he should sit on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs next to the heart; then take the spatulum, and cut into the skin between the ribs up to the breastbone, and make the incision straight while cutting into the skin of the ribs all the way to the white skin, and scrape gently according to his strength; then pierce the skin fully with water through a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then apply your fingers, and let the skin heal; and do not touch the heart, but only the skin; cut all around it carefully, or the water will return if you do not cut well; and if the egg jumps during your work, put it back in its place when you have finished the work on the skin; then sew together the two lips of the skin of the ribs with one stitch, then heal it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the wound corrupted by another disease, then you must tie off the vessels that are suspended, fearing the flow of blood; then cut into the vein at the suspension, and extract the wound, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And if the water is collected in two parts together, you know that they are two blisters; then cover the other part as you did the first equally, then wash the blood, and put on the wound soft lamb's wool moistened with rose oil; and put another piece of lamb's wool moistened with wine and oil over it, and place a cloth over the two blisters, and place doubled linen over that, and bind it around all the length which is according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two pieces of cloth and stuff them with lamb's wool according to this appearance, and have them sewn together at the crotch of the breeches, and one of the shoulders press upon the bottom up to the back, and the other on the part of the hip; and the other two ends above the two angles, and have all the binding gathered in the buckle of the breeches; and sometimes this blister is treated with cautery in place of an iron incision, and it is that you press the thin chisel-like cautery upon the skin of the blisters, and it is heated as we have said so that the white pus containing the water is exposed; then take the cautery according to this form and pierce that pus at the joints, and scorch it with this thin hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And cut in all the ways you can, as long as you stretch everything out; and be careful that the fire doesn't touch the egg; and know that this work is safer; and move carefully to prevent blood loss, and avoid wounds from cutting; and if anything opposes you, whether an abscess, or bleeding, or something else, then cure what opposes you, according to what was said earlier.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this treatment due to its horribleness, then bring about a perforation as I told you, and when you are sure that the fluid has been drained from the egg, have the patient sit on a raised seat; then pierce the abscess in the lower part to the full width of the spathomile, and insert the perforation deeply into the body; make the holes wide so that all the fluid can flow out; then put cotton over the wound, and bandage it, and leave it for the rest of the fluid to drain, and then cure the wound until it is healed; and if the white membrane does not allow the fluid to exit through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat hydrocephalus patients, of which the shape has been described earlier; widen the wound, and know that the fluid will return and will be discharged six months later or about that time, and when it is discharged as before, and thus the patient will pass their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	Know that in the dissection of this armpit there are many dispositions of fear, because of which it seems better to leave it as it is. And I will tell you about its work and the similarities of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I therefore say that many abscesses come from the body, and especially in the groin; and this is through a great variety of cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is known as an excess of bitterness and ague, which is spread in the joints, or from a blow; and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body; and it does not hurt, and it is a serious abscess; and sometimes there are grey, fearful, and piercing abscesses with flowing color, and sometimes it comes from the vein, or inflammation of the vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is from the vein, it is known by the hot disposition of the abscess when you press it with your fingers; and you should not touch it.Si li apostemes s’asseient sur les gues, si est de nout d’artere et est grive maladi.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	Those who are affected by swelling of the vein are known by their appearance and the feeling of the fingers, and anyone can well judge the nature of this condition and similar ones; you should press on the heart of the testicles, then the egg is pushed up, and the white sac is drawn out from under the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the egg has become soft with these new characters, then you should therefore draw out the egg and squeeze it; and if there is air in the sac, or anything in the vessels inside, you should release all that tissue and squeeze it firmly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the origin of the yolk is at the back, then you must cut it completely and extract the yolk, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is done, employ the wound with moist wool in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is a kind of abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to an onion, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient suffers greatly when it moves; and the cure for this disease is just as fearsome as the one before, and yet we will tell you about its treatment according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	It is necessary for you to make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then bind the suspensory of the testicles with a towel, and all the vessels that are close to the penis, and tie them tightly; then cut through the spatumile in a broad, straight line across the vessels, so that they are exposed, and then cut from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples; then insert a needle with a double thread where the vein has appeared, and tie it to the first place where the vein came out, and then tie it directly to the other end; then draw them gently according to the length of the body, along with the corrupted moisture; then treat the wound as we have said for the others, or insert a bow so that some vessels may be cut that nourish one of the testicles; for there is no harm in this, and if the vein appears in all the vessels, it is necessary to draw the testicles to all the vessels, so that the ureter does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and dry out and can no longer help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rot of the scrotum
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The causes of this hernia are either by the incision that comes from the scrotum, or the extension above the abdomen in the region of the groin, causing the intestines to descend through this opening to one of the testicles; and this opening is either in the scrotum, or from the extension of it, and these two types of hernia come about for many reasons: from a blow, or a jump, or a strain, or the lifting of a heavy load, and similar things; and the sign that it is an extension from the scrotum is that it happens gradually over a long time, and does not occur suddenly; and the abscesses are even all the way to the bottom, because the scrotum presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are that it is of the section of the syphilis, that it brings sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear various, under the skin close by, and it is due to the exit of the intestine and the body from the syphilis.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the stones descend with the intestine, and are retained inside, and cause great pain for the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments of iron, there is fear, because of which one should abstain from it.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	And the way to treat it is to instruct the patient to pull the intestine back into the wound with his hand if he can; then hold the scrotum between your hands and lift the testes; then press the abdomen above, and grasp all the skin of the testicles from their long end; then insert a pair of forceps into the opening of the scrotum according to what you need in order to open the wound, so that the bile can come out; then cut away the scrotum under the skin of the testicles, until all the hard white scrotum is exposed on all sides; then put your index finger into that which follows the testicle, in that which is between the white scrotum that is under the skin of the egg, and between the second scrotum, and away from that which is behind the egg, and between the second scrotum; then move your right hand inside the scrotum, and hold the white scrotum up in your left hand, and lift the egg up with all the scrotum towards the abdomen; and instruct the assistant to extend the egg upward, and untie that which is behind the bandage; and feel with your fingers if there is any intestine wrapped around the hard white scrotum, and if you find anything, pull it back into the abdomen; then take a needle through which there is a thick thread made from ten fibers, and insert it through the back part of the scrotum, which is after the skin of the testicles; then grab the ends of the threads with your fingers, so that there are four threads; then tie them together in a cross shape, and bind the scrotum, of which we have spoken that is under the skin of the testicles, with a strong ligature in two places; then wrap around the threads and tie them tightly in two places, so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter and cause an abscess to form; then put the ligature according to the first long ligature, two fingers from it; and after these two ligatures leave the scrotum that is under the skin of the testicles with the greater part of a finger; and after all this, grab in the part that is under the skin of the testicles, as far as the blood vessels and the skin, as we have said before; then apply soft wool soaked in oil to the wounds, and apply the ligature that we have described.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, due to fear of blood flow.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	For this happens many times, and leave the bandage on until it bites through; and if it is slow to fall off, then soak it in hot water, and apply what we have said again, until it falls off; then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the ancients say that it is made like the ram's horn which is together with the vein, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after the incision above slightly under; then press on it gently, and treat the abscess with what we have said, until the vessels fall away; then cure it as we have said, until it is perfectly healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres; et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent; et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert; et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois; et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre; puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines; puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Sometimes a fistula occurs in the veins, as we have said, and it opens up; and no intestines come out into the anus, and if they do, it is very little, and you must mend them every hour; and even if it remains too long in this state, then the wound becomes putrid, so that the intestines come out; and this happens by the extension of the pus into the veins, as we have said, for it is extended, then made soft and swollen, and opens up; and its cure is by cautery, as we have said before; and sometimes it is cured by iron in this way: and you must let the patient lie on his back between your hands, then press on the swollen area of the fistula with a large amount of salt according to the size of an egg; then draw out the pus which is under the skin that surrounds the anus, then take a needle and place it over the visible part of the fistula; then press it firmly into the depth of the abdomen, then cut the two visible parts of the fistula on the needle, and cut one and the other; then draw out the head of the needle, and do not cover or extend the wound in any way, as I have made you aware in the cure for a fistula of the intestines; then cure it with the cure for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the thread, clean and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	Syrup is constricting and has no appearance in bleeding, and cautery is more beneficial and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the scrotum becomes soft in some men because the testicles inside are softened, and it appears milky white; and when one wishes to treat it, they must make the patient lie on his back, and cut the softened skin on top of the natural skin; then sew the two lips together with a single stitch, and if you see, close the superfluity of the softened skin with three or four stitches firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it as other wounds until it heals, and cut the thread.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	You should know that castration is prohibited in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to discuss it in this book. It is only necessary for two reasons: the first is so that the doctors can answer questions and know how to treat the condition; the second is because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as bulls, rams, horses, and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	I say therefore that castration is done in two ways: by menarik, or by cutting.Si il est fait par atraction, il faille prendre et li testicules et li cordons et les attraire vers le bas tant qu’il soient deffaitz; et s’il ne peut ataindre a li testicules, qu’il tire li cordons tant qu’il soit adessis, et qu’il ne se muevent plus; car il ne faut que l’atraction soit faicte selonc la nature des cordons.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	In that which we do by attraction, we make the beast sit in warm water until its joints are softened and relaxed; then you grip it with your hand, until it is healed and you no longer feel anything.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	On castration: you must dye the beast and press its testicles in your left hand, then tie the scrotum, and beat each testicle one by one when you have well-scratched them; and leave some pus of the syphilitic medicine and the subtle syphilitic medicine which is on the vessels; and this type of castration is better than that done by attraction, because with attraction something may remain in the testicles, causing the beast to desire lust; then cure the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	Hermaphroditism in men occurs in two ways: one is that between the two testicles appears as the form of nature of a woman, and it has hair, and sometimes urinate from it.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other way is in women, and it has above the wrist as well as a wand and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.
